# <a name="windows-installer-error-messages-for-developers"></a><span data-ttu-id="5b7c4-104">針對開發人員 Windows Installer 的錯誤訊息 () </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5b7c4-104">Windows Installer Error Messages (for Developers)</span></span>

> [!NOTE]  
> <span data-ttu-id="5b7c4-105">本文適用于使用 Windows Installer 為其應用程式建立安裝程式套件的軟體發展人員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5b7c4-105">This article is intended for software developers who are using Windows Installer to build installer packages for their applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5b7c4-106">如果您是在安裝或卸載應用程式期間或之後遇到電腦問題的使用者，請洽詢客戶對您嘗試安裝或移除之軟體的支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5b7c4-106">If you are a user experiencing difficulty with your computer either during or after installing or uninstalling an application, contact customer support for the software you are trying to install or remove.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5b7c4-107">如果您覺得您需要支援 Microsoft 產品，請前往我們的技術支援網站，網址為 [support.microsoft.com](https://support.microsoft.com)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5b7c4-107">If you feel you are in need of support for a Microsoft product, please go to our technical support site at [support.microsoft.com](https://support.microsoft.com).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5b7c4-108">本主題詳述的錯誤碼是由 Windows Installer 傳回，錯誤碼為1000或更新版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5b7c4-108">The error codes detailed in this topic are returned by the Windows Installer, and have error codes of 1000 or greater.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5b7c4-109">編號1000到1999的錯誤碼會送出錯誤，而且必須撰寫到 [錯誤資料表](error-table.md)中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5b7c4-109">The error codes numbered 1000 to 1999 are ship errors and must be authored into the [Error table](error-table.md).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5b7c4-110">編號大於2000的錯誤碼是內部錯誤，不會有撰寫的字串，但如果安裝套件未正確撰寫，則可能會發生這些錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5b7c4-110">The error codes numbered greater than 2000 are internal errors and do not have authored strings, but these can occur if the installation package has been incorrectly authored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5b7c4-111">如需 Windows Installer 函式特定的錯誤碼 **MsiExec.exe** 和 **InstMsi.exe**，請參閱 [MsiExec.exe 和 InstMsi.exe 錯誤訊息](error-codes.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5b7c4-111">For error codes specific to the Windows Installer functions **MsiExec.exe** and **InstMsi.exe**, see [MsiExec.exe and InstMsi.exe Error Messages](error-codes.md).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5b7c4-112">如需保留的錯誤碼清單，請參閱 [錯誤資料表](error-table.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5b7c4-112">For a list of reserved error codes, see [Error table](error-table.md).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5b7c4-113">您可以搜尋網際網路或 [Microsoft 支援服務網站](https://support.microsoft.com/) ，以取得下表中許多訊息的解決方案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5b7c4-113">You can search the Internet or the [Microsoft support site](https://support.microsoft.com/) for solutions to many of the messages in the following table.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5b7c4-114">安裝套件的開發人員也可以使用內部一致性評估工具來測試其套件的內部一致性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5b7c4-114">Developers of installation packages can also test the internal consistency of their packages by using Internal Consistency Evaluators.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5b7c4-115">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [內部一致性評估工具-ices-003](internal-consistency-evaluators-ices.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5b7c4-115">For more information, see [Internal Consistency Evaluators - ICEs](internal-consistency-evaluators-ices.md).</span></span>
